<template>
  <button @click="increment">
    Count is: {{ state.count }}, double is: {{ state.double }}
  </button>
</template>

<script>
  import { reactive, computed } from 'vue'

  export default {
    setup() {
      const state = reactive({
        count: 0,
        double: computed(() => state.count * 2),
      })

      function increment() {
        state.count++
      }

      return {
        state,
        increment,
      }
    },
  }
</script>

æ‰‹æ’•ä»£ç 

2020-03-23
Offer / å­—èŠ‚è·³åŠ¨

é¢è¯•ä¸“é¢˜æ€»ç»“ï¼šæ‰‹æ’•ä»£ç 

å¸Œæœ›è¯»è€…ä¾æ­¤æ„å»ºè‡ªå·±çš„çŸ¥è¯†æ ‘ï¼ˆæ€ç»´å¯¼å›¾ï¼‰

å·æ‡’ä¸€ä¸‹ï¼šå¯å‚è€ƒæˆ‘è‡ªå·±æ€»ç»“æ€ç»´å¯¼å›¾ : ç‚¹è¿™é‡Œ

æ‰‹æ’•ä»£ç åœ°å€ï¼šåœ°å€

é™„å¸¦ï¼šé«˜é¢‘é¢è¯•é¢˜ç§¯ç´¯æ–‡æ¡£ã€‚ æ¥è‡ªäºï¼ˆå­¦é•¿ã€ç‰›å®¢ç½‘ç­‰å¹³å°ï¼‰

è‡ªå·±å¼€å‘çš„åšå®¢åœ°å€ï¼šzxinc520.com

github åœ°å€: ç‚¹å‡»

æ­¤ç¯‡ js - ã€æ‰‹æ’•ä»£ç ã€‘ çŸ¥è¯†ç‚¹ï¼š å…¨éƒ¨å¼„æ‡‚äº†ï¼Œé¢è¯•å¾ˆå®¹æ˜“ã€‚

1ã€Promiseï¼ˆA+è§„èŒƒï¼‰ã€thenã€all æ–¹æ³•

/*
     Promiseï¼šæ„é€  Promise å‡½æ•°å¯¹è±¡
     excutor: æ‰§è¡Œæ„é€ å™¨ ï¼ˆåŒæ­¥æ‰§è¡Œï¼‰
*/
function Promise(excutor) {
  const _that = this;
  _that.status = "pending"; // ç»™ promiseå¯¹è±¡æŒ‡å®š statuså±æ€§,åˆå§‹å€¼ä¸º pending
  _that.data = undefined; //ç»™ promise å¯¹è±¡æŒ‡å®šä¸€ä¸ªç”¨äºå‚¨å­˜ç»“æœæ•°æ®çš„å±æ€§
  _that.callbacks = []; // æ¯ä¸ªå…ƒç´ çš„ç»“æ„ï¼š{ onFulfilled(){}, onRejected(){}}

  function resolve(value) {
    // å¦‚æœå½“å‰çŠ¶æ€ä¸æ˜¯ pendingï¼Œç›´æ¥ç»“æŸ
    if (_that.status !== "pending") return;

    // å°† çŠ¶æ€æ”¹ä¸º resolved
    _that.status = "resolved";

    // ä¿å­˜ value æ•°æ®
    _that.data = value;

    // å¦‚æœæœ‰å¾…æ‰§è¡Œcallback å‡½æ•°ï¼Œç«‹åˆ»å¼‚æ­¥æ‰§è¡Œå›è°ƒå‡½æ•°
    if (_that.callbacks.length > 0) {
      setTimeout(() => {
        _that.callbacks.forEach((callbacksObj) => {
          callbacksObj.onFulfilled(value);
        });
      });
    }
  }

  function reject(reason) {
    // å¦‚æœå½“å‰çŠ¶æ€ä¸æ˜¯ pendingï¼Œç›´æ¥ç»“æŸ
    if (_that.status !== "pending") return;

    // å°† çŠ¶æ€æ”¹ä¸º rejected
    _that.status = "rejected";

    // ä¿å­˜ value æ•°æ®
    _that.data = reason;

    // å¦‚æœæœ‰å¾…æ‰§è¡Œcallback å‡½æ•°ï¼Œç«‹åˆ»å¼‚æ­¥æ‰§è¡Œå›è°ƒå‡½æ•°
    if (_that.callbacks.length > 0) {
      setTimeout(() => {
        _that.callbacks.forEach((callbacksObj) => {
          callbacksObj.onRejected(reason);
        });
      });
    }
  }

  //ç«‹åˆ»åŒæ­¥æ‰§è¡Œ excutor
  try {
    excutor(resolve, reject);
  } catch (error) {
    //å¦‚æœæ‰§è¡Œå™¨æŠ›å‡ºå¼‚å¸¸ï¼Œpromiseå¯¹è±¡å˜ä¸º rejected çŠ¶æ€
    reject(error);
  }
}

/*
          PromiseåŸå‹å¯¹è±¡çš„ then() --- *æ€è·¯*

            1ã€æŒ‡å®šæˆåŠŸå’Œå¤±è´¥çš„å›è°ƒå‡½æ•°
            2ã€è¿”å›ä¸€ä¸ªæ–°çš„ promise å¯¹è±¡
            3ã€è¿”å›promiseçš„ç»“æœç”± onFulfilled/onRejectedæ‰§è¡Œç»“æœå†³å®š
            4ã€æŒ‡å®š onFulfilled/onRejectedçš„é»˜è®¤å€¼
         */
Promise.prototype.then = function (onFulfilled, onRejected) {
  onFulfilled =
    typeof onFulfilled === "function" ? onFulfilled : (reason) => reason; //å‘åä¼ é€’æˆåŠŸçš„value

  //æŒ‡å®šé»˜è®¤çš„å¤±è´¥çš„å›è°ƒï¼ˆå®ç°é”™è¯¯/å¼‚å¸¸ç©¿é€çš„å…³é”®ç‚¹ï¼‰
  onRejected =
    typeof onRejected === "function"
      ? onRejected
      : (reason) => {
          //å‘åä¼ é€’å¤±è´¥çš„reason
          throw reason;
        };

  const _that = this;

  //è¿”å›ä¸€ä¸ªæ–°çš„promise å¯¹è±¡
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    /*
                    è°ƒç”¨æŒ‡å®šçš„å›è°ƒå‡½æ•°å¤„ç†ï¼Œæ ¹æ®æ‰§è¡Œç»“æœï¼Œæ”¹å˜returnçš„promiseçš„çŠ¶æ€
                 */
    function handle(callback) {
      /*
                           1. å¦‚æœæŠ›å‡ºå¼‚å¸¸ï¼Œreturn çš„promiseå°±ä¼šå¤±è´¥ï¼Œreason å°±æ˜¯ error
                           2. å¦‚æœå›è°ƒå‡½æ•°è¿”å›çš„ä¸æ˜¯promiseï¼Œreturnçš„promiseå°±ä¼šæˆåŠŸï¼Œvalueå°±æ˜¯è¿”å›çš„å€¼
                           3.å¦‚æœå›è°ƒå‡½æ•°è¿”å›çš„æ˜¯promiseï¼Œreturnçš„promiseçš„ç»“æœå°±æ˜¯è¿™ä¸ªpromiseçš„ç»“æœ
                        */

      try {
        const result = callback(_that.data);

        // 3.å¦‚æœå›è°ƒå‡½æ•°è¿”å›çš„æ˜¯promiseï¼Œreturnçš„promiseçš„ç»“æœå°±æ˜¯è¿™ä¸ªpromiseçš„ç»“æœ
        if (result instanceof Promise) {
          // result.then(
          //     value => resolve(value), //å½“resultæˆåŠŸæ—¶ï¼Œè®©returnçš„promiseä¹ŸæˆåŠŸ
          //     reason => reject(reason)  //å½“resultå¤±è´¥æ—¶ï¼Œè®©returnçš„promiseä¹Ÿå¤±è´¥
          // )

          result.then(resolve, reject);
        } else {
          //  2. å¦‚æœå›è°ƒå‡½æ•°è¿”å›çš„ä¸æ˜¯promiseï¼Œreturnçš„promiseå°±ä¼šæˆåŠŸï¼Œvalueå°±æ˜¯è¿”å›çš„å€¼
          resolve(result);
        }
      } catch (error) {
        //1. å¦‚æœæŠ›å‡ºå¼‚å¸¸ï¼Œreturn çš„promiseå°±ä¼šå¤±è´¥ï¼Œreason å°±æ˜¯ error

        reject(error);
      }
    }

    if (_that.status === "pending") {
      //å‡è®¾å½“å‰çŠ¶æ€è¿˜æ˜¯ pending çŠ¶æ€ï¼Œå°†å›è°ƒå‡½æ•° ä¿å­˜èµ·æ¥
      _that.callbacks.push({
        onFulfilled(value) {
          handle(onFulfilled); //æ”¹promiseçš„çŠ¶æ€ä¸º onFulfilledçŠ¶æ€
        },
        onRejected(reason) {
          handle(onRejected); //æ”¹promiseçš„çŠ¶æ€ä¸º onRejectedçŠ¶æ€
        },
      });
    } else if (_that.status === "resolved") {
      //å¦‚æœå½“å‰æ˜¯resolvedçŠ¶æ€ï¼Œå¼‚æ­¥æ‰§è¡Œonresolvedå¹¶æ”¹å˜returnçš„promiseçŠ¶æ€
      setTimeout(() => {
        handle(onFulfilled);
      });
    } else {
      //onRejected
      setTimeout(() => {
        //å¦‚æœå½“å‰æ˜¯rejectedçŠ¶æ€ï¼Œå¼‚æ­¥æ‰§è¡ŒonRejectedå¹¶æ”¹å˜returnçš„promiseçŠ¶æ€
        handle(onRejected);
      });
    }
  });
};

/*
            PromiseåŸå‹å¯¹è±¡çš„ catch()
            æŒ‡å®šå¤±è´¥çš„å›è°ƒå‡½æ•°
            è¿”å›ä¸€ä¸ªæ–°çš„ promise å¯¹è±¡
         */
Promise.prototype.catch = function (onRejected) {
  return this.then(undefined, onRejected);
};

Promise.prototype.finally = function (callback) {
  return this.then(
    (value) => {
      Promise.resolve(callback(value));
    },
    (reason) => {
      Promise.resolve(callback(reason));
    }
  );
};

/*
            Promiseå‡½æ•°å¯¹è±¡çš„ resolve()
            è¿”å› æŒ‡å®šç»“æœçš„ "æˆåŠŸ" çš„ promise å¯¹è±¡
         */
Promise.resolve = function (value) {
  //è¿”å› ä¸€ä¸ª æˆåŠŸ/å¤±è´¥ çš„promise
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    if (value instanceof Promise) {
      //ä½¿ç”¨valueçš„ç»“æœä½œä¸º promise çš„ç»“æœ
      value.then(resolve, reject);
    } else {
      //valueä¸æ˜¯promise => promiseå˜ä¸ºæˆåŠŸï¼Œæ•°æ®æ˜¯ value
      resolve(value);
    }
  });
};

/*
            Promiseå‡½æ•°å¯¹è±¡çš„ reject()
            è¿”å› æŒ‡å®šç»“æœçš„ "å¤±è´¥" çš„ promise å¯¹è±¡
         */
Promise.reject = function (reason) {
  //è¿”å› ä¸€ä¸ªå¤±è´¥çš„ promise
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    reject(reason);
  });
};

/*
            Promiseå‡½æ•°å¯¹è±¡çš„ all()
            è¿”å› ä¸€ä¸ªpromiseï¼Œåªæœ‰å½“æ‰€æœ‰promiseéƒ½æˆåŠŸæ—¶æ‰æˆåŠŸï¼Œå¦åˆ™åªè¦æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªå¤±è´¥å°± å¤±è´¥
         */
Promise.all = function (promises) {
  const values = Array.apply(null, { length: promises.length }); //ç”¨æ¥ä¿å­˜æ‰€æœ‰æˆåŠŸ valueçš„æ•°ç»„
  let resolvedCount = 0;

  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    //éå†è·å–æ¯ä¸€ä¸ª promiseçš„ç»“æœ
    promises.forEach((p, index) => {
      Promise.resolve(p).then(
        //pæˆåŠŸï¼Œå°†æˆåŠŸçš„ value ä¿å­˜ values
        // values.push(value)  => ä¸èƒ½è¿™æ ·
        (value) => {
          resolvedCount++; //æˆåŠŸçš„æ¬¡æ•°

          values[index] = value;

          //å¦‚æœå…¨éƒ¨æˆåŠŸäº†ï¼Œå°†returnçš„ promise æ”¹ä¸ºæˆåŠŸ
          if (resolvedCount === promises.length) {
            resolve(values);
          }
        },
        (reason) => {
          //åªè¦ä¸€ä¸ªå¤±è´¥äº†ï¼Œreturn çš„promiseå°±å¤±è´¥
          reject(reason);
        }
      );
    });
  });
};

/*
            Promiseå‡½æ•°å¯¹è±¡çš„ race()
            è¿”å› ä¸€ä¸ªpromiseï¼Œå…¶ç»“æœç”±ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå®Œæˆçš„promiseæ¥å†³å®š
         */
Promise.race = function (promises) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    //éå†è·å–æ¯ä¸€ä¸ª promiseçš„ç»“æœ
    promises.forEach((p, index) => {
      Promise.resolve(p).then(
        (value) => {
          // ä¸€æ—¦ç”±æˆåŠŸäº†ï¼Œå°†return å˜ä¸ºå¤±è´¥
          resolve(value);
        },

        (reason) => {
          //åªè¦ä¸€ä¸ªå¤±è´¥äº†ï¼Œreturn çš„promiseå°±å¤±è´¥
          reject(reason);
        }
      );
    });
  });
};

2ã€æ‰‹å†™ call apply bind

// è‡ªå®šä¹‰applyå‡½æ•°
Function.prototype.apply1 = function (obj, arg) {
  //contextä¸ºnullæˆ–è€…æ˜¯undefinedæ—¶,è®¾ç½®é»˜è®¤å€¼
  if (!obj) {
    obj = typeof window === "undefined" ? global : window;
  }
  obj.fn = this;
  let result = null;
  //undefined æˆ–è€… æ˜¯ null ä¸æ˜¯ Iterator å¯¹è±¡ï¼Œä¸èƒ½è¢« ...
  if (arg === undefined || arg === null) {
    result = obj.fn(arg);
  } else {
    result = obj.fn(...arg);
  }
  delete obj.fn;
  return result;
};

// è‡ªå®šä¹‰ call å‡½æ•°
Function.prototype.call1 = function (obj, ...arg) {
  if (!obj) {
    obj = typeof window === "undefined" ? global : window;
  }
  obj.fn = this;
  let result = null;
  result = obj.fn(...arg);
  delete obj.fn;
  return result;
};

// è‡ªå®šä¹‰ bind å‡½æ•°
Function.prototype.bind = function (obj, ...arg) {
  if (!obj) {
    obj = typeof window === "undefined" ? global : window;
  }
  let self = this;
  let args = arg;

  function f() {}

  f.prototype = this.prototype;
  let bound = function () {
    let res = [...args, ...arguments];
    let obj = this instanceof f ? this : obj;
    return self.apply(obj, res);
  };
  bound.prototype = new f();
  return bound;
};

3ã€Promise å°è£… Ajax æ–¹æ³•

function ajax(url, methods, data) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    let xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
    xhr.open(methods, url, true);
    xhr.send(data);
    xhr.onreadystatechange = function () {
      if (xhr.readyState === 4 && xhr.status === 200) {
        resolve(xhr.responseText);
      } else {
        reject(xhr.status);
      }
    };
  });
}

4ã€å¼‚æ­¥åŠ è½½å›¾ç‰‡

function loadImageAsync(url) {
  return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
    const image = new Image();
    image.onload = function () {
      resolve(image);
    };
    image.onerror = function () {
      reject(new Error("Could not load image at " + url));
    };
    image.src = url;
  });
}

5ã€é˜²æŠ–ï¼ŒèŠ‚æµ

//é˜²æŠ–
function debounce(fn, delay) {
  let timeout = null;
  return function () {
    clearTimeout(timeout);
    timeout = setTimeout(() => {
      fn.apply(this, arguments);
    }, delay);
  };
}

//èŠ‚æµ
function throttle(fn, delay) {
  let canRun = true;
  return function () {
    if (!canRun) return;
    canRun = false;
    setTimeout(() => {
      fn.apply(this, arguments);
      canRun = true;
    }, delay);
  };
}

    function inheritPrototype(subType, superType) {

8ã€è‡ªå®šä¹‰ new è¿‡ç¨‹

function _new(fn, ...arg) {
  let obj = {};
  obj.__proto__ = fn.prototype;
  let ret = fn.apply(obj, arg);
  return ret instanceof Object ? ret : obj;
}

9ã€æ‰‹å†™é€’å½’æ–¹æ³•å®ç°æ·±æ‹·è´

// æ‰‹å†™å®ç°æ·±æ‹·è´
function checkedType(target) {
  return Object.prototype.toString.call(target).slice(8, -1);
}

function clone(target) {
  let targrtType = checkedType(target);
  let result = null;
  if (targrtType === "Object") {
    result = {};
  } else if (targrtType === "Array") {
    result = [];
  } else {
    return target;
  }
  for (let item in target) {
    let value = target[item];
    if (checkedType(value) === "Object" || checkedType(value) === "Array") {
      result[item] = clone(value);
    } else {
      result[item] = value;
    }
  }
  return result;
}

10ã€å®ç°ä¸€ä¸ªæŸ¯é‡ŒåŒ–å‡½æ•°

//ES5å†™æ³•
const currying = function (fn, ...args) {
  if (args.length < fn.length) {
    return function () {
      return currying(fn, ...args, ...arguments);
    };
  } else {
    return fn(...args);
  }
};

//ES6å†™æ³•
const currying = (fn, ...args) =>
  args.length < fn.length
    ? (...argments) => currying(fn, ...args, ...argments)
    : fn(...args);

      get: function () {
        return obj[key];
      },
      set: function (newvalue) {
        obj[key] = newvalue;

    });
  }
}

10ã€JS å‘å¸ƒè®¢é˜…æ¨¡å¼

let pubSub = {
  list: {},
  subscribe: function (key, fn) {
    //è®¢é˜…
    if (!this.list[key]) {
      this.list[key] = [];
    }
    this.list[key].push(fn);
  },
  publish: function (key, ...args) {
    //å‘å¸ƒ
    for (let fn of this.list[key]) {
      fn.apply(this, args);
    }
  },
  unSubscribe: function (key, fn) {
    //å–æ¶ˆè®¢é˜…
    let fnlist = this.list[key];
    if (!fnlist) return;
    if (!fn) {
      fnlist.length = 0;
    } else {
      fnlist.forEach((item, index) => {
        if (item === index) {
          fnlist.splice(index, 1);
        }
      });
    }
  },
};

pubSub.subscribe("onwork", (time) => {
  console.log(`ä¸Šç­äº†ï¼š${time}`);
});
pubSub.subscribe("offwork", (time) => {
  console.log(`ä¸‹ç­äº†ï¼š${time}`);
});
pubSub.subscribe("launch", (time) => {
  console.log(`åƒé¥­äº†ï¼š${time}`);
});

// // å‘å¸ƒ
pubSub.publish("offwork", "18:00:00");
pubSub.publish("launch", "12:00:00");

pubSub.unSubscribe("onwork");
pubSub.publish("onwork", "1222:00:00");

//1ã€æ±‚äºŒå‰æ ‘ä¸­çš„èŠ‚ç‚¹ä¸ªæ•°
function getNodenum(root) {
  if (root == null) {
    return;
  }
  return getNodenum(root.left) + getNodenum(root.right) + 1;
}

//2ã€æ±‚äºŒå‰æ ‘çš„æœ€å¤§æ·±åº¦
function maxDepth(root) {
  if (root == null) {
    return;
  }
  return Math.max(maxDepth(root.left), maxDepth(root.right)) + 1;
}

//3.äºŒå‰æ ‘çš„æœ€å°æ·±åº¦
function minDepth(root) {
  if (root == null) return;
  let left = minDepth(root.left);
  let right = minDepth(root.right);
  return left == 0 || right == 0 ? left + right + 1 : Math.min(left, right) + 1;
}

//4.å…ˆåºéå†ï¼ˆé€’å½’ï¼‰
function preroot(root, callback) {
  if (root != null) {
    callback(root.key);
    preroot(root.left, callback);
    preroot(root.right, callback);
  }
}

//å…ˆåºéå†ï¼ˆéé€’å½’ï¼‰
function preroot(root) {
  let stack = [],
    result = [];
  if (root != null) {
    stack.push(root);
  }
  while (stack.length != 0) {
    let temp = stack.pop();
    result.push(temp.key);

    if (temp.left != null) {
      stack.push(temp.left);
    }
    if (temp.right != null) {
      stack.push(temp.right);
    }
  }
  return result;
}

//5 ä¸­åºéå†ï¼ˆé€’å½’ï¼‰
function middleroot(root, callback) {
  if (root != null) {
    preroot(root.left, callback);
    callback(root.key);
    preroot(root.right, callback);
  }
}

//5.1 ä¸­åºéå†ï¼ˆéé€’å½’ï¼‰
function middleroot(root) {
  let stack = [],
    result = [];
  while (true) {
    while (root != null) {
      stack.push(root);
      root = root.left;
    }
    if (stack.length == 0) {
      break;
    }
    let temp = stack.pop();
    result.push(temp.key);
    stack.push(temp.right);
  }
  return result;
}

//åˆ†å±‚éå†ï¼ˆé€’å½’ï¼‰
function bfs(root) {
  let queue = [],
    result = [];
  let pointer = 0;
  if (root != null) {
    queue.push(root);
  }
  let bfsFun = function () {
    let temp = queue[pointer];
    if (temp) {
      result.push(temp.key);
      if (temp.left) {
        queue.push(temp.left);
      }
      if (temp.right) {
        queue.push(temp.right);
      }
      pointer++;
      bfsFun();
    }
  };
  bfsFun();
  return result;
}

//åˆ†å±‚éå†ï¼ˆéé€’å½’ï¼‰
function bfs(root) {
  let queue = [],
    result = [];
  if (root !== null) {
    queue.push(root);
  }
  let pointer = 0;
  while (pointer < queue.length) {
    let temp = queue[pointer++];
    result.push(temp.key);
    temp.left && queue.push(temp.left);
    temp.right && queue.push(temp.right);
  }
  return result;
}

function zhiRoot(root) {
  let stack1 = [],
    stack2 = [],
    result = [];

  if (root != null) {
    stack1.push(root);
  }
  let flag = 1;
  while (stack1.length != 0 || stack2.length != 0) {
    const list = [];
    if (flag % 2) {
      while (stack1.length != 0) {
        let temp = stack2.pop();
        list.push(temp.key);
        temp.left && stack2.push(temp.left);
        temp.right && stack2.push(temp.right);
      }
    } else {
      while (stack2.length != 0) {
        let temp = stack1.pop();
        list.push(temp.key);
        temp.left && stack1.push(temp.left);
        temp.right && stack1.push(temp.right);
      }
    }
    i++;
    result.push(list);
  }
  return result;
}

function Print(root) {
  const result = [];

  if (root === null) {
    return result;
  }

  const stack1 = [];
  const stack2 = [];

  stack1.push(root);
  let flag = 1;
  while (stack1.length !== 0 || stack2.length !== 0) {
    const list = [];
    if (flag % 2) {
      while (stack1.length !== 0) {
        const temp = stack2.pop();
        list.push(temp.val);
        temp.left && stack2.push(temp.left);
        temp.right && stack2.push(temp.right);
      }
    } else {
      while (stack2.length !== 0) {
        const temp = stack1.pop();
        list.push(tmp.val);
        temp.left && stack1.push(temp.left);
        temp.right && stack1.push(temp.right);
      }
    }
    i++;
    result.push(list);
  }
  return result;
}

//7ã€æ±‚äºŒå‰æ ‘ç¬¬Kå±‚çš„èŠ‚ç‚¹ä¸ªæ•°
function getknum(root, k) {
  if (root == null || k < 0) {
    return;
  }
  if (root !== null && k == 1) {
    return 1;
  }
  return getknum(root.left, k - 1) + getknum(root.right, k - 1);
}

//8.æ±‚äºŒå‰æ ‘ç¬¬Kå±‚çš„å¶å­èŠ‚ç‚¹ä¸ªæ•°
function getksonnum(root, k) {
  if (root == null || k < 0) {
    return;
  }
  if (root != null && k == 1) {
    if (root.left == null && root.right == null) {
      return 1;
    } else {
      return 0;
    }
  }
  return getksonnum(root, k - 1) + getksonnum(root, k - 1);
}

//åè½¬äºŒå‰æ ‘
function reverseRoot(root) {
  if (root == null) {
    return;
  }
  let temp = root.left;
  root.left = reverseRoot(root.right);
  root.right = reverseRoot(temp);
  return root;
}

// æ±‚äºŒå‰æ ‘çš„ç›´å¾„
function longerlength(root) {
  let path = 0;
  getlongerlength(root);
  return path;

  function getlongerlength(root) {
    if (root == null) {
      return;
    }
    let left = longerlength(root.left);
    let right = longerlength(root.right);
    path = Math.max(path, left + right);
    return Math.max(left, right) + 1;
  }
}

// äºŒå‰æ ‘ä¸­å’Œä¸ºæŸä¸€å€¼çš„è·¯å¾„
function getPath(root, target) {
  let result = [];
  if (root) {
    findPath(root, target, [], 0, result);
  }
  return result;

  function findPath(root, target, stack, sum, result) {
    stack.push(root.key);
    sum += root.key;
    if (!root.left && !root.right && sum === target) {
      result.push(stack.slice(0));
    }
    if (root.left) {
      findPath(root.left, target, stack, sum, result);
    }
    if (root.right) {
      findPath(root.right, target, stack, sum, result);
    }
    stack.pop();
  }
}

//ç»™å®šä¸€æ£µäºŒå‰æœç´¢æ ‘ï¼Œè¯·æ‰¾å‡ºå…¶ä¸­çš„ç¬¬kå°çš„ç»“ç‚¹ã€‚(ä¸­åºéå†+ kå°)

13ã€å®ç°ä¸€ä¸ªé“¾è¡¨

function linkedList() {
  function node(data) {
    this.data = data;
    this.next = null;
  }

  this.head = null;
  this.length = 0;

  linkedList.prototype.append = function (data) {
    let newnode = new node(data);
    if (this.head == null) {
      this.head = newnode;
    } else {
      let current = this.head;
      while (current.next) {
        current = current.next;
      }
      current.next = newnode;
      this.length++;
    }
  };
  linkedList.prototype.find = function (data) {
    let current = this.head;
    while (current.next) {
      if (current.data === data) {
        break;
      }
      current = current.next;
    }
    return current;
  };

  linkedList.prototype.fixed = function (data, newdata) {
    let current = this.find(data);
    current.data = newdata;
  };

  linkedList.prototype.prefind = function (data) {
    let current = this.head;
    while (current.next) {
      if (current.next.data === data) {
        break;
      }
      current = current.next;
    }
    return current;
  };

  linkedList.prototype.delete = function (data) {
    if (this.head.data === data) {
      this.head = this.head.next;
      return;
    }
    let prenode = this.prefind(data);
    let current = this.find(data);
    prenode = current.next;
  };

  linkedList.prototype.toString = function () {
    let result = "";
    let current = this.head;
    while (current) {
      result += current.data + "->";
      current = current.next;
    }
    return result;
  };
}
let a = new linkedList();
a.append("abc");
a.append("abcd");
a.append("abcde");
console.log(a.toString());

a.fixed("abc", 11111);
console.log(a.toString());

//é“¾åœ°å€æ³•
//è£…è½½å› å­ï¼ˆ0.25ï¼Œ0.75ï¼‰
function HashTable() {
  //å±æ€§
  this.storage = []; //å­˜å‚¨çš„ä½ç½®
  this.count = 0; // æ•°ç›®
  this.limit = 7; //æœ€ç»ˆé™åˆ¶æ•°ç»„çš„å¤§å°

  //æ–¹æ³•
  // å“ˆå¸Œå‡½æ•°
  HashTable.prototype.hashFunc = function (str, size) {
    //1ã€å®šä¹‰ hashCodeå˜é‡
    let hashCode = 0;
    for (let i = 0; i < str.length; i++) {
      //2ã€éœçº³ç®—æ³•ï¼Œæ¥è®¡ç®—hashCodeçš„å€¼
      hashCode = 37 * hashCode + str.charCodeAt(i);
    }
    //3ã€å–ä½™æ“ä½œ
    let index = hashCode % size;
    return index;
  };

  //æ’å…¥&ä¿®æ”¹æ“ä½œ
  HashTable.prototype.put = function (key, value) {
    //1.æ ¹æ®keyè·å–å¯¹åº”çš„ index
    let index = this.hashFunc(key, this.limit);
    // 2ã€æ ¹æ® index å–å‡ºå¯¹åº”çš„ bucket
    let bucket = this.storage[index];

    //3ã€åˆ¤æ–­ bucketæ˜¯å¦ä¸ºç©º
    if (bucket == null) {
      bucket = [];
      this.storage[index] = bucket;
    }
    //4ã€åˆ¤æ–­æ˜¯å¦æ˜¯ä¿®æ”¹æ•°æ®
    for (let i = 0; i < bucket.length; i++) {
      let tuple = bucket[i];
      if (tuple[0] == key) {
        tuple[1] = value;
        return;
      }
    }
    //5.æ·»åŠ æ“ä½œ
    bucket.push([key, value]);
    this.count++;

    //åˆ¤æ–­æ˜¯å¦éœ€è¦æ‰©å®¹
    if (this.count > this.limit * 0.75) {
      this.resize(this.limit * 2);
    }
  };

  //è·å–æ“ä½œ
  HashTable.prototype.get = function (key) {
    let index = this.hashFunc(key, this.limit);
    let bucket = this.storage[index];
    if (bucket == null) {
      return false;
    }
    for (let i = 0; i < bucket.length; i++) {
      let tuple = bucket[i];
      if (tuple[0] === key) {
        return tuple[1];
      }
    }
  };
  HashTable.prototype.remove = function (key) {
    let index = this.hashFunc(key, this.limit);
    let bucket = this.storage[index];
    if (bucket == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (let i = 0; i < bucket.length; i++) {
      let tuple = bucket[i];
      if (tuple[0] == key) {
        bucket.splice(i, 1);
        this.count--;

        //ç¼©å°å®¹é‡
        if (this.limit > 7 && this.count < this.limit * 0.75) {
          this.resize(Math.floor(this.limit / 2));
        }

        return tuple[1];
      }
    }
    return null;
  };

  //å“ˆå¸Œè¡¨çš„æ‰©å®¹ã€
  HashTable.prototype.resize = function (newLimit) {
    //1.ä¿å­˜æ—§çš„æ•°æ®å†…å®¹
    let oldStorage = this.storage;
    //2. é‡ç½®æ‰€æœ‰çš„å±æ€§

    this.storage = [];
    this.count = 0;
    this.limit = newLimit;

    //3.éå† oldStorage æ‰€æœ‰çš„ bucket
    for (let i = 0; i < oldStorage.length; i++) {
      let bucket = oldStorage[i];
      if (bucket == null) {
        continue;
      }
      for (let j = 0; j < bucket.length; j++) {
        let tuple = bucket[i];
        this.put(tuple[0], tuple[1]);
      }
    }
  };
}
let a = new HashTable();
a.put("zc", "15");
a.put("zc1", "115");
a.put("z1", "115");
a.put("asd", "115");
a.put("wew", "115");
a.remove("wew");
console.log(a.get("wew"));

function Queue() {
  //æ ˆä¸­çš„å±æ€§
  this.items = [];

  //1.å‹å…¥æ ˆpush()
  Queue.prototype.enqueue = function (...element) {
    this.items.push(...element);
  };

  //2.ä»é˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸­åˆ é™¤å‰ç«¯å…ƒç´ 
  Queue.prototype.dequeue = function () {
    return this.items.shift();
  };

  //3.æŸ¥çœ‹ä¸€ä¸‹å‰ç«¯å…ƒç´ 
  Queue.prototype.front = function () {
    return this.items[0];
  };

  //4.åˆ¤æ–­æ ˆæ˜¯å¦ä¸ºç©º
  Queue.prototype.isEmpty = function () {
    return this.items.length === 0;
  };
  //5.è·å–æ ˆä¸­å…ƒç´ çš„ä¸ªæ•°
  Queue.prototype.size = function () {
    return this.items.length;
  };
  //6.toStringæ–¹æ³•
  Queue.prototype.toString = function () {
    return this.items.toString().split(",").join(" ");
  };
}

function Graph() {
  //å±æ€§ï¼š é¡¶ç‚¹ï¼ˆæ•°ç»„ï¼‰/è¾¹ï¼ˆå­—å…¸ï¼‰
  this.vertexes = []; //é¡¶ç‚¹
  this.edges = new Map(); //è¾¹

  //æ–¹æ³•
  //å¢åŠ å¯¹åº”é¡¶ç‚¹çš„æ–¹æ³•
  Graph.prototype.addVertex = function (v) {
    this.vertexes.push(v);
    this.edges.set(v, []);
  };

  Graph.prototype.addEdge = function (v1, v2) {
    this.edges.get(v1).push(v2);
    this.edges.get(v2).push(v1);
  };

  //å®ç°toString æ–¹æ³•
  Graph.prototype.toString = function () {
    //å®šä¹‰å­—ç¬¦è½¬ï¼Œä¿å­˜æœ€ç»ˆçš„ç»“æ„
    let resultString = "";
    for (let i = 0; i < this.vertexes.length; i++) {
      resultString += this.vertexes[i] + "->";
      let vEdges = this.edges.get(this.vertexes[i]);
      for (let j = 0; j < vEdges.length; j++) {
        resultString += vEdges[j] + " ";
      }
      resultString += "\n";
    }
    return resultString;
  };

  //å›¾çš„éå†

  //åˆå§‹åŒ–çŠ¶æ€é¢œè‰²
  Graph.prototype.initializeColor = function () {
    let colors = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < this.vertexes.length; i++) {
      colors[this.vertexes[i]] = "white";
    }
    return colors;
  };

  //å¹¿åº¦ä¼˜å…ˆæœç´¢ç®—æ³•(BFS)  åŸºäºé˜Ÿåˆ—å®Œæˆ
  Graph.prototype.bfs = function (initV, handler) {
    //1.åˆå§‹åŒ–é¢œè‰²
    let colors = this.initializeColor();

    //2.åˆ›å»ºé˜Ÿåˆ—
    let queue = new Queue();

    //3.å°†é¡¶ç‚¹åŠ å…¥é˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸­
    queue.enqueue(initV);

    //4.å¾ªç¯ä»é˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸­å–å‡ºå…ƒç´ 
    while (!queue.isEmpty()) {
      // 4.1ä»é˜Ÿåˆ—å–å‡ºä¸€ä¸ªé¡¶ç‚¹
      let v = queue.dequeue();

      //4.2 è·å–å’Œé¡¶ç‚¹ç›¸è¿çš„å¦å¤–é¡¶ç‚¹
      let vList = this.edges.get(v);

      //4.3 å°†vçš„é¢œè‰²è®¾ç½®ä¸ºç°è‰²
      colors[v] = "gray";

      //4.4  éå†æ‰€æœ‰çš„é¡¶ç‚¹ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”åŠ å…¥åˆ°é˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸­
      for (let i = 0; i < vList.length; i++) {
        let e = vList[i];
        if (colors[e] == "white") {
          colors[e] = "gray";
          queue.enqueue(e);
        }
      }

      //4.5 è®¿é—®é¡¶ç‚¹
      handler(v);

      //4.6 å°†é¡¶ç‚¹è®¾ç½®ä¸ºé»‘è‰²
      colors[v] = "black";
    }
  };

  //å¹¿åº¦ä¼˜å…ˆæœç´¢ç®—æ³•ï¼ˆDFSï¼‰
  Graph.prototype.dfs = function (initV, handler) {
    let colors = this.initializeColor();

    //é€’å½’è®¿é—®
    this.dfsVisit(initV, colors, handler);
  };

  Graph.prototype.dfsVisit = function (v, colors, handler) {
    //1.å°†é¢œè‰²è®¾ç½®ä¸ºç°è‰²
    colors[v] = "gray";
    //2.å¤„ç†VèŠ‚ç‚¹
    handler(v);

    //3.è®¿é—®vç›¸è¿çš„é¡¶ç‚¹
    let vList = this.edges.get(v);
    for (let i = 0; i < vList.length; i++) {
      let e = vList[i];
      if (colors[e] === "white") {
        this.dfsVisit(e, colors, handler);
      }
    }

    //4.å°†vè®¾ç½®ä¸ºé»‘è‰²
    colors[v] = "black";
  };
}

16ã€å‡ ç§æ’åºç®—æ³•çš„å®ç°

function ArrayList() {
  this.array = [];

  ArrayList.prototype.insert = function (item) {
    this.array.push(item);
  };

  ArrayList.prototype.toString = function () {
    return this.array.join("-");
  };

  ArrayList.prototype.swap = function (m, n) {
    let temp = this.array[m];
    this.array[m] = this.array[n];
    this.array[n] = temp;
  };
  //å®ç°æ’åºç®—æ³•
  //å†’æ³¡æ’åº
  ArrayList.prototype.bubbles = function () {
    if (this.array === null || this.array.length < 2) return this.array;
    let length = this.array.length;
    for (let i = length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      for (let j = 0; j < i; j++) {
        if (this.array[j] > this.array[j + 1]) {
          this.swap(j, j + 1);
        }
      }
    }
  };

  //é€‰æ‹©æ’åº
  ArrayList.prototype.selectSort = function () {
    if (this.array === null || this.array.length < 2) return this.array;
    let length = this.array.length;
    for (let i = 0; i < length - 1; i++) {
      let min = i;
      for (let j = i + 1; j < length; j++) {
        if (this.array[min] > this.array[j]) {
          min = j;
        }
      }
      this.swap(min, i);
    }
  };

  //æ’å…¥æ’åº
  ArrayList.prototype.insertSort = function () {
    if (this.array === null || this.array.length < 2) return this.array;
    let length = this.array.length;

    for (let i = 1; i < length; i++) {
      var temp = this.array[i];
      let j = i;
      while (this.array[j - 1] > temp && j > 0) {
        this.array[j] = this.array[j - 1];
        j--;
      }
      this.array[j] = temp;
    }
  };

  //é«˜çº§æ’åº
  //å¸Œå°”æ’åº (å¯¹æ’å…¥æ’åºçš„å‡çº§)
  ArrayList.prototype.shellSort = function () {
    if (this.array === null || this.array.length < 2) return this.array;
    let length = this.array.length;
    //åˆå§‹åŒ–å¢é‡
    var gap = Math.floor(length / 2);
    // whlieå¾ªç¯
    while (gap > 1) {
      for (let i = gap; i < length; i++) {
        let temp = this.array[i];
        let j = i;
        while (this.array[j - gap] > temp && j > gap - 1) {
          this.array[j] = this.array[j - gap];
          j -= gap;
        }
        this.array[j] = temp;
      }
      gap = Math.floor(gap / 2);
    }
  };
}
// å¿«æ’
function median(arr, left, right) {
  let center = Math.floor(left + (right - left) / 2);
  if (arr[left] > arr[center]) {
    swap(arr, left, right);
  }
  if (arr[center] > arr[right]) {
    swap(arr, center, right);
  }
  if (arr[left] > arr[right]) {
    swap(arr, left, right);
  }
  swap(center, right - 1);
  return arr[right - 1];
}
function swap(arr, m, n) {
  let temp = arr[m];
  arr[m] = arr[n];
  arr[n] = temp;
}
function quickSort(arr) {
  if (arr.length <= 1) {
    return arr;
  }
  return quickSortFun(arr, 0, arr.length - 1);
}
function quickSortFun(arr, left, right) {
  if (left < right) {
    let pivot = median(arr, left, right);
    let i = 0;
    let j = right - 1;
    while (true) {
      while (arr[++i] < pivot) {}
      while (arr[--j] > pivot && j > left) {}
      if (i < j) {
        swap(arr, i, j);
      } else {
        break;
      }
    }
    if (i < right) {
      swap(arr, i, right - 1);
    }
    quickSortFun(arr, left, i - 1);
    quickSortFun(arr, i + 1, right);
  }
  return arr;
}
console.log(quickSort([1, 4, 2, 3, 1]));

console.log(it.next());
console.log(it.next());

function makeIterator(array) {
  let nextindex = 0;
  return {
    next: function () {
      if (nextindex < array.length) {
        return { value: array[nextindex++], done: false };
      } else {
        return { value: undefined, done: true };
      }
    },
  };
}

// function getNum(arr) {

function getNum(arr) {
  let max = 0;
  let sum = 0;
  for (let num of arr) {
    if (sum < 0) {
      sum = 0;
    }
    sum += num;
    max = Math.max(max, sum);
  }
  return max;
}

console.log(getNum(arr));

19ã€å®ç°ä¸€ä¸ª EventListener ç±»ï¼ŒåŒ…å« onï¼Œoffï¼Œemit æ–¹æ³•

//å®ç°ä¸€ä¸ªEventListenerç±»ï¼ŒåŒ…å«onï¼Œoffï¼Œemitæ–¹æ³•
class EventListener {
  constructor() {
    this.list = {};
  }

  on(key, fn) {
    if (!this.list[key]) {
      this.list[key] = [];
    }
    this.list[key].push(fn);
  }

  emit(key, ...args) {
    for (let fn of this.list[key]) {
      fn.apply(this, args);
    }
  }

  off(key, fn) {
    let fnlist = this.list[key];
    if (!fnlist) return;
    if (!fn) {
      fnlist.length = 0;
    } else {
      fnlist.forEach((item, index) => {
        if (item === fn) {
          fnlist.splice(index, 1);
        }
      });
    }
  }
}

let obj1 = new EventListener();

obj1.on("work", (value) => {
  console.log(`æˆ‘æ˜¯${value}å•Š`);
});

obj1.on("eat", (value) => {
  console.log(`æˆ‘åœ¨${value}å•Š`);
});

obj1.emit("work", "zc");

obj1.off("eat");

obj1.emit("eat", "åƒè¥¿ç“œ");

function getnum(num) {
  if (num <= 1) return 1;
  return getnum(num - 1) + getnum(num - 2);
}
console.log(getnum(2));
// ----------------------------------

//åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’
function getnum(n) {
  let temp = [];
  if (n == 1 || n == 2) {
    return 1;
  } else {
    temp[1] = 1;
    temp[2] = 2;
    for (let i = 3; i < n; i++) {
      temp[i] = temp[i - 1] + temp[i - 2];
    }
    return temp[i - 1];
  }
}

22ã€åªåŒ…å«â€™(â€˜, â€˜)â€™, â€˜[â€˜, â€˜]â€™, â€˜{â€˜, â€˜}â€™ çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œåˆ¤æ–­æ˜¯å¦æœ‰æ•ˆã€‚

var isValid = function (s) {
  var rightSymbols = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
    if (s[i] == "(") {
      rightSymbols.push(")");
    } else if (s[i] == "{") {
      rightSymbols.push("}");
    } else if (s[i] == "[") {
      rightSymbols.push("]");
    } else if (rightSymbols.pop() != s[i]) {
      return false;
    }
  }
  return !rightSymbols.length;
};

let arr = [1, [1, [3], 2], 2, [1], 3, 4];
let count = 0;

function getDep(arr) {
  let p = false;
  p = arr.some((item) => {
    return item.length > 0;
  });

  if (p) {
    count++;
    getDep(arr.flat());
  } else {
    return count;
  }
}
console.log(getDep(arr));

let arr = [1, 2, 3, 2, [2, 3], [2, [1], 2]];
function wrap() {
  let ret = [];
  return function flatten(arr) {
    for (let item of arr) {
      if (item.constructor === Array) {
        ret.concat(flatten(item));
      } else {
        ret.push(item);
      }
    }
    return ret;
  };
}
console.log(wrap()(arr));

26ã€æ¨¡æ‹Ÿ js ç²¾åº¦ä¸¢å¤±é—®é¢˜

IEEE 754 æ ‡å‡†

function add(num1, num2) {
  const num1Digits = (num1.toString().split(".")[1] || "").length;
  const num2Digits = (num2.toString().split(".")[1] || "").length;
  const baseNum = Math.pow(10, Math.max(num1Digits, num2Digits));
  return (num1 * baseNum + num2 * baseNum) / baseNum;
}
console.log(add(0.1, 0.2));

    return instance || (instance = new singleTon(name));

})();

let getInstance = (function () {
  let instance = null;
  return function (name) {
    if (!instance) {
      this.name = name;
      return (instance = this);
    }
    return instance;
  };
})();

const getSingle = function (fn) {

// ç›®æ ‡è€…ç±»
class Subject {
  constructor() {
    this.observers = []; // è§‚å¯Ÿè€…åˆ—è¡¨
  }
  // æ·»åŠ 
  add(observer) {
    this.observers.push(observer);
  }

  // åˆ é™¤
  remove(observer) {
    let idx = this.observers.findIndex((item) => item === observer);
    idx > -1 && this.observers.splice(idx, 1);
  }

  // é€šçŸ¥
  notify() {
    for (let observer of this.observers) {
      observer.update();
    }
  }
}

// è§‚å¯Ÿè€…ç±»
class Observer {
  constructor(name) {
    this.name = name;
  }

  // ç›®æ ‡å¯¹è±¡æ›´æ–°æ—¶è§¦å‘çš„å›è°ƒ
  update() {
    console.log(`ç›®æ ‡è€…é€šçŸ¥æˆ‘æ›´æ–°äº†ï¼Œæˆ‘æ˜¯ï¼š${this.name}`);
  }
}

// å®ä¾‹åŒ–ç›®æ ‡è€…
let subject = new Subject();

// å®ä¾‹åŒ–ä¸¤ä¸ªè§‚å¯Ÿè€…
let obs1 = new Observer("å‰ç«¯å¼€å‘è€…");
let obs2 = new Observer("åç«¯å¼€å‘è€…");

// å‘ç›®æ ‡è€…æ·»åŠ è§‚å¯Ÿè€…
subject.add(obs1);
subject.add(obs2);

// ç›®æ ‡è€…é€šçŸ¥æ›´æ–°
subject.notify();
// è¾“å‡ºï¼š
// ç›®æ ‡è€…é€šçŸ¥æˆ‘æ›´æ–°äº†ï¼Œæˆ‘æ˜¯å‰ç«¯å¼€å‘è€…
// ç›®æ ‡è€…é€šçŸ¥æˆ‘æ›´æ–°äº†ï¼Œæˆ‘æ˜¯åç«¯å¼€å‘è€…

class Receiver {

    console.log("æ¥æ”¶è€…æ‰§è¡Œè¯·æ±‚");
  }

class Command {

  constructor(receiver) {
    this.receiver = receiver;
  }
  execute() {
    // è°ƒç”¨æ¥æ”¶è€…å¯¹åº”æ¥å£æ‰§è¡Œ
    console.log("å‘½ä»¤å¯¹è±¡->æ¥æ”¶è€…->å¯¹åº”æ¥å£æ‰§è¡Œ");
    this.receiver.execute();

}

    this.command = command;

    // å‘å¸ƒè¯·æ±‚ï¼Œè°ƒç”¨å‘½ä»¤å¯¹è±¡
    console.log("å‘å¸ƒè€…å‘å¸ƒè¯·æ±‚");
    this.command.execute();
  }
}

const fs = require("fs");
const path = require("path");

const readfile = function (filename) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    fs.readFile(path.join(__dirname, filename), "utf-8", function (
      error,
      data
    ) {
      if (error) return reject(error);
      resolve(data);
    });
  });
};

readfile("./01.txt")
  .then((value) => {
    console.log(value);
    return readfile("./02.txt");
  })
  .then((value) => {
    console.log(value);
    return readfile("./03.txt");
  })
  .then((value) => {
    console.log(value);
  })
  .catch((reason) => {
    console.log(reason);
  });

const readfile = function (filename) {

    function ajaxGet(url, callback) {
  var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
  xhr.open("GET", url, true);
  xhr.send();

  xhr.onreadystatechange = function () {
    if (xhr.readyState == 4 && xhr.status == 200) {
      callback(xhr.responseText);
    }
  };
}

20ã€ Iterator å’Œ forâ€¦ofï¼ˆIterator éå†å™¨çš„å®ç°ï¼‰

function makeiterator(arr) {
  var nextindex = 0;
  return {
    next: function () {
      return nextindex < arr.length
        ? { value: arr[nextindex++], done: false }
        : { value: undefined, done: true };
    },
  };
}
// Symbol.iteratoréå†å™¨æ¥å£
let arr = ["a", "b", "c"];
let iter = arr[Symbol.iterator]();

iter.next(); // { value: 'a', done: false }
iter.next(); // { value: 'b', done: false }
iter.next(); // { value: 'c', done: false }

  //contextä¸ºnullæˆ–è€…æ˜¯undefinedæ—¶,è®¾ç½®é»˜è®¤å€¼

    Function.prototype.call1 = function (obj, ...arg) {
  if (!obj) {
    obj = typeof window === "undefined" ? global : window;
  }
  obj.fn = this;
  let result = null;
  result = obj.fn(...arg);
  delete obj.fn;
  return result;
};

    Function.prototype.bind1 = function (obj, ...arg) {
  if (!obj) {
    obj = typeof window === "undefined" ? global : window;
  }
  let self = this;
  let args = arg;
  function f() {}
  f.prototype = this.prototype;
  let bound = function () {
    let res = [...args, ...arguments];
    let _this = this instanceof f ? this : obj;
    return self.apply(_this, res);
  };
  bound.prototype = new f();
  return bound;
};
